\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{gd\_info()}{gd\_info()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily gd\+\_\+info (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Retrieve information about the currently installed GD library \mbox{\hyperlink{patch2_8txt_a3f9992ab8fa942ed02faa63682c3a84c}{array an associative array. }} 

\tabulinesep=1mm
\begin{longtabu}spread 0pt [c]{*{0}{|X[-1]}|}
\hline
\end{longtabu}
of array returned by {\bfseries{gd\+\_\+info}} 

Attribute 

Meaning  

GD Version 

string value describing the installed libgd version.  

Free\+Type Support 

boolean value. {\bfseries{T\+R\+UE}} if Free\+Type Support is installed.  

Free\+Type Linkage 

string value describing the way in which Free\+Type was linked. Expected values are\+: \textquotesingle{}with freetype\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}with T\+TF library\textquotesingle{}, and \textquotesingle{}with unknown library\textquotesingle{}. This element will only be defined if Free\+Type Support evaluated to {\bfseries{T\+R\+UE}}.  

T1\+Lib Support 

boolean value. {\bfseries{T\+R\+UE}} if T1\+Lib support is included.  

G\+IF Read Support 

boolean value. {\bfseries{T\+R\+UE}} if support for reading G\+IF images is included.  

G\+IF Create Support 

boolean value. {\bfseries{T\+R\+UE}} if support for creating G\+IF images is included.  

J\+P\+EG Support 

boolean value. {\bfseries{T\+R\+UE}} if J\+P\+EG support is included.  

P\+NG Support 

boolean value. {\bfseries{T\+R\+UE}} if P\+NG support is included.  

W\+B\+MP Support 

boolean value. {\bfseries{T\+R\+UE}} if W\+B\+MP support is included.  

X\+BM Support 

boolean value. {\bfseries{T\+R\+UE}} if X\+BM support is included.  

WebP Support 

boolean value. {\bfseries{T\+R\+UE}} if WebP support is included.  

Previous to P\+HP 5.\+3.\+0, the J\+P\+EG Support attribute was named J\+PG Support. \begin{DoxySince}{Since}
4.\+3 

5.\+0 
\end{DoxySince}

Return an image containing the affine tramsformed src image, using an optional clipping area \mbox{\hyperlink{patch2_8txt_a3f9992ab8fa942ed02faa63682c3a84c}{resource \$image }}An image resource, returned by one of the image creation functions, such as \mbox{\hyperlink{patch2_8txt_a3f9992ab8fa942ed02faa63682c3a84c}{imagecreatetruecolor()}}.

\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
resource$\vert$bool Return affined image resource on success or F\+A\+L\+SE on failure.

\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
The two images will be merged according to pct which can range from 0 to 100. When pct = 0, no action is taken, when 100 this function behaves identically to imagecopy for pallete images, while it implements alpha transparency for true colour images.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{imagecreatefrombmp()}{imagecreatefrombmp()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily imagecreatefrombmp (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$filename }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

{\bfseries{\mbox{\hyperlink{gd_8php_ae31d5b4cff1e502fb0c51505e67e3e9a}{imagecreatefrombmp()}}}} returns an image identifier representing the image obtained from the given filename. {\bfseries{T\+IP}} \mbox{\hyperlink{class_a}{A}} U\+RL can be used as a filename with this function if the fopen wrappers have been enabled. See \{\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\mbox{\hyperlink{standard__5_8php_a8b216a61fe5b78054003f5ee8580481d}{fopen()}}\} for more details on how to specify the filename. See the Supported Protocols and Wrappers for links to information about what abilities the various wrappers have, notes on their usage, and information on \mbox{\hyperlink{phpunit_2phpunit_2src_2_framework_2_assert_2_functions_8php_aa950afcee01981fe0485ce00ff0e8e8c}{any}} predefined variables they may provide. 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
string & {\em \$filename} & Path to the B\+MP image. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
resource$\vert$false Returns an image resource identifier on success, {\bfseries{F\+A\+L\+SE}} on errors. \mbox{\hyperlink{patch2_8txt_a3f9992ab8fa942ed02faa63682c3a84c}{7.\+2 }}
\end{DoxyReturn}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily imageftbbox (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$size,  }\item[{}]{\$angle,  }\item[{}]{\$fontfile,  }\item[{}]{\$text,  }\item[{}]{\$extrainfo = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{_core__d_8php_afa4c647ecaee0da639b8549bb3abf62b}{null}}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Give the bounding box of a text using fonts via freetype2 \mbox{\hyperlink{patch2_8txt_a3f9992ab8fa942ed02faa63682c3a84c}{float \$size }} The font size. Depending on your version of GD, this should be specified as the pixel size (G\+D1) or point size (G\+D2).

\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}

\end{DoxyParams}

Depending on which version of the GD library that P\+HP is using, it may attempt to search for files that do not begin with a leading \textquotesingle{}/\textquotesingle{} by appending \textquotesingle{}.ttf\textquotesingle{} to the filename and searching along a library-\/defined font path.

Meaning

Defines drawing linespacing  

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
array$\vert$false imageftbbox returns an array with 8 elements representing four points making the bounding box of the text\+: 
\end{DoxyReturn}


0 

lower left corner, X position  

1 

lower left corner, Y position  

2 

lower right corner, X position  

3 

lower right corner, Y position  

4 

upper right corner, X position  

5 

upper right corner, Y position  

6 

upper left corner, X position  

7 

upper left corner, Y position  

The points are relative to the text regardless of the angle, so \char`\"{}upper left\char`\"{} means in the top left-\/hand corner seeing the text horizontally. Returns false on error. \begin{DoxySince}{Since}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{imagefttext()}{imagefttext()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily imagefttext (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$image,  }\item[{}]{\$size,  }\item[{}]{\$angle,  }\item[{}]{\$x,  }\item[{}]{\$y,  }\item[{}]{\$color,  }\item[{}]{\$fontfile,  }\item[{}]{\$text,  }\item[{}]{\$extrainfo = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{_core__d_8php_afa4c647ecaee0da639b8549bb3abf62b}{null}}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Write text to the image using fonts using Free\+Type 2 \mbox{\hyperlink{patch2_8txt_a3f9992ab8fa942ed02faa63682c3a84c}{resource \$image  float \$size }} The font size to use in points. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
float & {\em \$angle} & \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
The angle in degrees, with 0 degrees being left-\/to-\/right reading text. Higher values represent a counter-\/clockwise rotation. For example, a value of 90 would result in bottom-\/to-\/top reading text. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
int & {\em \$x} & \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
The coordinates given by x and y will define the basepoint of the first character (roughly the lower-\/left corner of the character). This is different from the imagestring, where x and y define the upper-\/left corner of the first character. For example, \char`\"{}top left\char`\"{} is 0, 0. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
int & {\em \$y} & \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
The y-\/ordinate. This sets the position of the fonts baseline, not the very bottom of the character. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
int & {\em \$color} & \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
The index of the desired color for the text, see imagecolorexact. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
string & {\em \$fontfile} & \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
The path to the True\+Type font you wish to use. 

Depending on which version of the GD library P\+HP is using, when fontfile does not begin with a leading / then .ttf will be appended to the filename and the library will attempt to search for that filename along a library-\/defined font path. 

When using versions of the GD library lower than 2.\+0.\+18, a space character, rather than a semicolon, was used as the \textquotesingle{}path separator\textquotesingle{} for different font files. Unintentional use of this feature will result in the warning message\+: Warning\+: Could not find/open font. For these affected versions, the only solution is moving the font to a path which does not contain spaces. 

In many cases where a font resides in the same directory as the script using it the following trick will alleviate any include problems. 


\begin{DoxyPre}
<?php
// Set the enviroment variable for GD
putenv('GDFONTPATH=' . realpath('.'));\end{DoxyPre}



\begin{DoxyPre}// Name the font to be used (note the lack of the .ttf extension)
\$font = 'SomeFont';
?>
\end{DoxyPre}
 $<$p$<$blockquote$>$

{\bfseries{Note\+:}} {\ttfamily open\+\_\+basedir} does {\itshape not} apply to fontfile. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
string & {\em \$text} & \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
Text to be inserted into image. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
array & {\em \$extrainfo} & \mbox{[}optional\mbox{]} \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\begin{longtabu}spread 0pt [c]{*{0}{|X[-1]}|}

\end{longtabu}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{imageloadfont()}{imageloadfont()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily imageloadfont (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$file }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Load a new font \mbox{\hyperlink{patch2_8txt_a3f9992ab8fa942ed02faa63682c3a84c}{string \$file }} The font file format is currently binary and architecture dependent. This means you should generate the font files on the same type of C\+PU as the machine you are running P\+HP on. 

\tabulinesep=1mm
\begin{longtabu}spread 0pt [c]{*{0}{|X[-1]}|}
\hline
\end{longtabu}
file format 

byte position 

C data type 

description  

byte 0-\/3 

int 

number of characters in the font  

byte 4-\/7 

int 

value of first character in the font (often 32 for space)   

byte 8-\/11 

int 

pixel width of each character  

byte 12-\/15 

int 

pixel height of each character  

byte 16-\/ 

char 

array with character data, one byte per pixel in each character, for a total of (nchars$\ast$width$\ast$height) bytes.   

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
int$\vert$false The font identifier which is always bigger than 5 to avoid conflicts with built-\/in fonts or false on errors. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

5.\+0 
\end{DoxySince}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{imagepstext()}{imagepstext()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily imagepstext (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$image,  }\item[{}]{\$text,  }\item[{}]{\$font\+\_\+index,  }\item[{}]{\$size,  }\item[{}]{\$foreground,  }\item[{}]{\$background,  }\item[{}]{\$x,  }\item[{}]{\$y,  }\item[{}]{\$space = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{_core__d_8php_afa4c647ecaee0da639b8549bb3abf62b}{null}}},  }\item[{}]{\$tightness = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{_core__d_8php_afa4c647ecaee0da639b8549bb3abf62b}{null}}},  }\item[{}]{\$angle = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{_core__d_8php_afa4c647ecaee0da639b8549bb3abf62b}{null}}},  }\item[{}]{\$antialias\+\_\+steps = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{_core__d_8php_afa4c647ecaee0da639b8549bb3abf62b}{null}}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Draws a text over an image using Post\+Script Type1 fonts \mbox{\hyperlink{patch2_8txt_a3f9992ab8fa942ed02faa63682c3a84c}{resource \$image  string \$text }} The text to be written. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
resource & {\em \$font\+\_\+index} & \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\mbox{\hyperlink{class_a}{A}} font resource, returned by imagepsloadfont. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
int & {\em \$size} & \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
size is expressed in pixels. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
int & {\em \$foreground} & \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
The color in which the text will be painted. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
int & {\em \$background} & \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
The color to which the text will try to fade in with antialiasing. No pixels with the color background are actually painted, so the background image does not need to be of solid color. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
int & {\em \$x} & \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
x-\/coordinate for the lower-\/left corner of the first character. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
int & {\em \$y} & \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
y-\/coordinate for the lower-\/left corner of the first character. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
int & {\em \$space} & \mbox{[}optional\mbox{]} \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
Allows you to change the default value of a space in a font. This amount is added to the normal value and can also be negative. Expressed in character space units, where 1 unit is 1/1000th of an em-\/square. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
int & {\em \$tightness} & \mbox{[}optional\mbox{]} \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
tightness allows you to control the amount of white space between characters. This amount is added to the normal character width and can also be negative. Expressed in character space units, where 1 unit is 1/1000th of an em-\/square. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
float & {\em \$angle} & \mbox{[}optional\mbox{]} \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
angle is in degrees. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
int & {\em \$antialias\+\_\+steps} & \mbox{[}optional\mbox{]} \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
Allows you to control the number of colours used for antialiasing text. Allowed values are 4 and 16. The higher value is recommended for text sizes lower than 20, where the effect in text quality is quite visible. With bigger sizes, use 4. It\textquotesingle{}s less computationally intensive. 

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
array$\vert$false This function returns an array containing the following elements\+: 
\end{DoxyReturn}


0 

lower left x-\/coordinate  

1 

lower left y-\/coordinate  

2 

upper right x-\/coordinate  

3 

upper right y-\/coordinate  Returns false on error. \begin{DoxySince}{Since}
4.\+0 

5.\+0 
\end{DoxySince}

\item[\mbox{\hyperlink{deprecated__deprecated000046}{Deprecated}}]7.\+0 This function was R\+E\+M\+O\+V\+ED in P\+HP 7.\+0.\+0. \end{DoxyRefDesc}

\index{gd.php@{gd.php}!imagesetinterpolation@{imagesetinterpolation}}
\index{imagesetinterpolation@{imagesetinterpolation}!gd.php@{gd.php}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{imagesetinterpolation()}{imagesetinterpolation()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily imagesetinterpolation (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$image,  }\item[{}]{\$method = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{gd_8php_a50a2da6f3e20213b2d9210206eb49d78}{I\+M\+G\+\_\+\+B\+I\+L\+I\+N\+E\+A\+R\+\_\+\+F\+I\+X\+ED}}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Set the interpolation method \mbox{\hyperlink{patch2_8txt_a3f9992ab8fa942ed02faa63682c3a84c}{resource \$image }} An image resource, returned by one of the image creation functions, such as \mbox{\hyperlink{patch2_8txt_a3f9992ab8fa942ed02faa63682c3a84c}{imagecreatetruecolor()}}. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
int & {\em \$method} & \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
The interpolation method, which can be one of the following\+: 
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item I\+M\+G\+\_\+\+B\+E\+LL\+: Bell filter.  
\item I\+M\+G\+\_\+\+B\+E\+S\+S\+EL\+: Bessel filter.  
\item I\+M\+G\+\_\+\+B\+I\+C\+U\+B\+IC\+: Bicubic interpolation.  
\item I\+M\+G\+\_\+\+B\+I\+C\+U\+B\+I\+C\+\_\+\+F\+I\+X\+ED\+: Fixed point implementation of the bicubic interpolation.  
\item I\+M\+G\+\_\+\+B\+I\+L\+I\+N\+E\+A\+R\+\_\+\+F\+I\+X\+ED\+: Fixed point implementation of the bilinear interpolation ({\itshape default (also on image creation)}).  
\item I\+M\+G\+\_\+\+B\+L\+A\+C\+K\+M\+AN\+: Blackman window function.  
\item I\+M\+G\+\_\+\+B\+OX\+: Box blur filter.  
\item I\+M\+G\+\_\+\+B\+S\+P\+L\+I\+NE\+: Spline interpolation.  
\item I\+M\+G\+\_\+\+C\+A\+T\+M\+U\+L\+L\+R\+OM\+: Cubbic Hermite spline interpolation.  
\item I\+M\+G\+\_\+\+G\+A\+U\+S\+S\+I\+AN\+: Gaussian function.  
\item I\+M\+G\+\_\+\+G\+E\+N\+E\+R\+A\+L\+I\+Z\+E\+D\+\_\+\+C\+U\+B\+IC\+: Generalized cubic spline fractal interpolation.  
\item I\+M\+G\+\_\+\+H\+E\+R\+M\+I\+TE\+: Hermite interpolation.  
\item I\+M\+G\+\_\+\+H\+A\+M\+M\+I\+NG\+: Hamming filter.  
\item I\+M\+G\+\_\+\+H\+A\+N\+N\+I\+NG\+: Hanning filter.  
\item I\+M\+G\+\_\+\+M\+I\+T\+C\+H\+E\+LL\+: Mitchell filter.  
\item I\+M\+G\+\_\+\+P\+O\+W\+ER\+: Power interpolation.  
\item I\+M\+G\+\_\+\+Q\+U\+A\+D\+R\+A\+T\+IC\+: Inverse quadratic interpolation.  
\item I\+M\+G\+\_\+\+S\+I\+NC\+: Sinc function.  
\item I\+M\+G\+\_\+\+N\+E\+A\+R\+E\+S\+T\+\_\+\+N\+E\+I\+G\+H\+B\+O\+UR\+: Nearest neighbour interpolation.  
\item I\+M\+G\+\_\+\+W\+E\+I\+G\+H\+T\+E\+D4\+: Weighting filter.  
\item I\+M\+G\+\_\+\+T\+R\+I\+A\+N\+G\+LE\+: Triangle interpolation.  
\end{DoxyItemize}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
bool Returns T\+R\+UE on success or F\+A\+L\+SE on failure. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxySince}{Since}
5.\+5 
\end{DoxySince}

\index{imagettfbbox@{imagettfbbox}!gd.php@{gd.php}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{imagettfbbox()}{imagettfbbox()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily imagettfbbox (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$size,  }\item[{}]{\$angle,  }\item[{}]{\$fontfile,  }\item[{}]{\$text }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Give the bounding box of a text using True\+Type fonts \mbox{\hyperlink{patch2_8txt_a3f9992ab8fa942ed02faa63682c3a84c}{float \$size }} The font size. Depending on your version of GD, this should be specified as the pixel size (G\+D1) or point size (G\+D2). 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
float & {\em \$angle} & \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
Angle in degrees in which text will be measured. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
string & {\em \$fontfile} & \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
The name of the True\+Type font file (can be a U\+RL). Depending on which version of the GD library that P\+HP is using, it may attempt to search for files that do not begin with a leading \textquotesingle{}/\textquotesingle{} by appending \textquotesingle{}.ttf\textquotesingle{} to the filename and searching along a library-\/defined font path. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
string & {\em \$text} & \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
The string to be measured. 

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
array$\vert$false imagettfbbox returns an array with 8 elements representing four points making the bounding box of the text on success and false on error. 
\end{DoxyReturn}


key 

contents  

0 

lower left corner, X position  

1 

lower left corner, Y position  

2 

lower right corner, X position  

3 

lower right corner, Y position  

4 

upper right corner, X position  

5 

upper right corner, Y position  

6 

upper left corner, X position  

7 

upper left corner, Y position  

The points are relative to the text regardless of the angle, so \char`\"{}upper left\char`\"{} means in the top left-\/hand corner seeing the text horizontally. \begin{DoxySince}{Since}
4.\+0 

5.\+0 
\end{DoxySince}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{gd_8php_aca11278546fdb7b00b45e75b5074e876}\label{gd_8php_aca11278546fdb7b00b45e75b5074e876}} 
\index{gd.php@{gd.php}!imagettftext@{imagettftext}}
\index{imagettftext@{imagettftext}!gd.php@{gd.php}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{imagettftext()}{imagettftext()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily imagettftext (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$image,  }\item[{}]{\$size,  }\item[{}]{\$angle,  }\item[{}]{\$x,  }\item[{}]{\$y,  }\item[{}]{\$color,  }\item[{}]{\$fontfile,  }\item[{}]{\$text }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Write text to the image using True\+Type fonts \mbox{\hyperlink{patch2_8txt_a3f9992ab8fa942ed02faa63682c3a84c}{resource \$image  float \$size }} The font size. Depending on your version of GD, this should be specified as the pixel size (G\+D1) or point size (G\+D2). 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
float & {\em \$angle} & \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
The angle in degrees, with 0 degrees being left-\/to-\/right reading text. Higher values represent a counter-\/clockwise rotation. For example, a value of 90 would result in bottom-\/to-\/top reading text. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
int & {\em \$x} & \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
The coordinates given by x and y will define the basepoint of the first character (roughly the lower-\/left corner of the character). This is different from the imagestring, where x and y define the upper-\/left corner of the first character. For example, \char`\"{}top left\char`\"{} is 0, 0. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
int & {\em \$y} & \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
The y-\/ordinate. This sets the position of the fonts baseline, not the very bottom of the character. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
int & {\em \$color} & \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
The color index. Using the negative of a color index has the effect of turning off antialiasing. See imagecolorallocate. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
string & {\em \$fontfile} & \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
The path to the True\+Type font you wish to use. 

Depending on which version of the GD library P\+HP is using, when fontfile does not begin with a leading / then .ttf will be appended to the filename and the library will attempt to search for that filename along a library-\/defined font path. 

When using versions of the GD library lower than 2.\+0.\+18, a space character, rather than a semicolon, was used as the \textquotesingle{}path separator\textquotesingle{} for different font files. Unintentional use of this feature will result in the warning message\+: Warning\+: Could not find/open font. For these affected versions, the only solution is moving the font to a path which does not contain spaces. 

In many cases where a font resides in the same directory as the script using it the following trick will alleviate any include problems. 


\begin{DoxyPre}
<?php
// Set the enviroment variable for GD
putenv('GDFONTPATH=' . realpath('.'));\end{DoxyPre}



\begin{DoxyPre}// Name the font to be used (note the lack of the .ttf extension)
\$font = 'SomeFont';
?>
\end{DoxyPre}
 $<$p$<$blockquote$>$

{\bfseries{Note\+:}} {\ttfamily open\+\_\+basedir} does {\itshape not} apply to fontfile. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
string & {\em \$text} & \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
The text string in U\+T\+F-\/8 encoding. 

May include decimal numeric character references (of the form\+: \&\#8364;) to access characters in a font beyond position 127. The hexadecimal format (like \&\#x\+A9;) is supported. Strings in U\+T\+F-\/8 encoding can be passed directly. 

Named entities, such as \&copy;, are not supported. Consider using html\+\_\+entity\+\_\+decode to decode these named entities into U\+T\+F-\/8 strings (\mbox{\hyperlink{standard__0_8php_ab16bade3af0ec4213d7bdfa5ad2bf720}{html\+\_\+entity\+\_\+decode()}} supports this as of P\+HP 5.\+0.\+0). 

If a character is used in the string which is not supported by the font, a hollow rectangle will replace the character. 

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
array$\vert$false an array with 8 elements representing four points making the bounding box of the text. The order of the points is lower left, lower right, upper right, upper left. The points are relative to the text regardless of the angle, so \char`\"{}upper left\char`\"{} means in the top left-\/hand corner when you see the text horizontally. Returns false on error. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxySince}{Since}
4.\+0 

5.\+0 
\end{DoxySince}
